TEbic yw teyrnas neuoeth i wr tuy / yr hwn aeth allan y bore glasdyth i

YR Ieshu a gymerth ato y deuthec / Luc. xviii.

gwynt a chwyth lle yr ewyllysa / a thy ae clywy of: eithyr ny wythost o ba le y
daw / nag y ba le ytha. Delly y may pop un a anet or yspryt. Nicodemus a
atebawth ac a thynot wrtho: Pa thelw y dychonhyn vot? Ieshu a atebawth ac a
thyuot wrtho: Awyt tiynathro in Israel ac ni wythog y petheu hynn? In wir / in
wir y doedaf wrthyt: y peth a wydam a thywedwn / ar peth a welsam a
testolaythwn: an testolayth ny derbyniwch. O threitheis i pethe dayarolion
ychwi / ac ny chredwch / pathelw o thraythaf ywch petheu nefolion / y
credwch-chwi? Ac nyd escennath nep ir nef / o thieithyr hwn a thescennath or
nef / is of map y dynyr hwn ye yd in y nef. A mal y dyrchavath Moysen y sarph
in y difieith / velly y ma'n their y vap y dyneu thyrchavael / ynny vo y pop un
a cred ynto of / na choler onid caffael bywyd tragyvythol.

Yr Euangel.
IEshu a thringawth yr llong ac a thaeth tros y mor / Mat. ix.
yw thinas ehunan. Ac well wy a thucsont ato wr arparlys / in gorweth mewn
gwely. Aphan welawth Ieshu y ffyth wy / e thyuot wrth y claf or paralys:
Ymthiriaid vap / cans die pechateu a vatheuir yty. A nycha y dwetson rei or gwyr
llen ynthunt euhunain: May hwn in caply. A phan welawth Ieshu eu methylieu e
dyuot: Paam y methyliwchi thrigio ni in ewch calonneu? Pa un hawsach e thywedyt
/ e vatheuwyt yty die pechate ae dywedyt / kyuot a roda? Ac er mwyn cahel o
hanoch wy bot vot gallu can vap y din y vatheu pechote ar y thayar: Yno y dyuot
of wrth y din ar parlys: Kyuot / a chymer die wely / a does yth tuy. Ac of a
gyuodes ac aeth yw duy. Agwedy gwelet or popul / wy a ryvethasont / ac a
roesont ogoniant i theo / pwy roesei ryw allu y thynion.

Mat. xviii.
PEtr a thyuot wrth Jesus: Arglwyth pa sawl gwa ith y matheuaf im brawd / pan
pecho in v'rbyn / ac hyd in seithwaith? Ac Ieshu a thyuot wrtho: Nyd wy v'yn
doedyt hyd seithwaith leithyr [hyd seithwaith dec a thruceinwaith. [sef
ebyilledi ne pa sawl gwaith bynac]
Ac am hynny y cyffelypir teyrnas nef i wr oeth in vrenhin / pwy a vynnei
gyfrif can eu weison. A phan thechreoth of cyfrif / e thucpwyt un ato oeth in y
thlet o thec mil o talenteu. A chan and oeth canto thim oeu taly / of
orchymynoth e Arglwyth ythynt y werthy of aeu wreic ae blant / a chymeint oll
oeth ar i elw / y wneuthy taledigaeth. Ar gwas hwnnw a syrthioth y lawr / ac a
atolygath itho can thoedyt: Aros arglwyth a byth tha ammy neth wrthyf / a mi a
dalaf yty y cwbyl oll. Ar arglwyth a trugarhath wrth y gwas hwnnw / ac ae
gollyngoth ac a vatheuoth y thlet. [hwnnw
Ar gwas [yma] aeth allan / ac a gavas un or gweison hynny oeth mal ynteu ehun
/ a hwn oeth in y thlet of o cant ceinoc / ac of a ymavloth ynto / ac ae
llindagoth can thoedyt: Tal die thlet. Ar gwas hwnnw a syrthyoth y lawr ac a
atolygawth itho can thoedyt: Aros / a byth tha die ymmyneth wrthyf a mi a dalaf
yt'y cwbyl oll. Ac of a wrthodws / ac ae danvonws of ir carcharduy / hyd any
thalei y thlet. A phan welath y gweison ereill y pe theu a wnaythit / yth oeth
in thrwc tras pen cantunt / ac a thaychant ac y vanegesont ew arglwyd yr holl
petheu a vefynt, Yno y galwoth eu arglwyth arno / ac e dyuot wr tho: Gwas y
Vall / well mi a vadeueis y ti yr oll thlet pan atoly geist yny: Ac anyd oeth
angenreidiol y ti trugathay wrth y gwas sith in gyffelyp yty / megys ac y
trugorhais i wrthyt ti? A llitio a wnaeth eu arglwyth / ac ae dodes of at y
poenwyr hyd a ny dalei yr oll thlet. Ac velly y gwna vymtat yr hwn sith in y
nevoeth y chwi any vathewch och calonneu (pop un yw vrawt) eu sarhaedeu.

ni welet y tat? A ny chredy vy mod i in y tat / ar tat yno vi? Y geirieu yth
wife in y traythy y chwi / nyd o honof vyhun yth wife in traythy. Y tat is id in
aros ynof / of e a wna y gweithredoeth. Credwch vy mod in y tat / ar tat yno
vi. A nyd e / er mwyn y gweithredoeth ehunain credwch vi. In wir / in wir mi a
thywedaf ychwi / hwn acred yno vi / y gweithredoeth ac a wnaf vi a wnaiff ynte
hevyt: a rei mwy na rey'n a wnaiff / can vy mod i in mynet at y tat. A pha peth
bynac a ovynnoch in v'en wi hyny a wnaf / any bo gogoniant ir tat t trw' yr
map. O gofynnwch thim in v'enw i / myvy ae gwnelwyf.

bot and oes onit amser byr itho.

Can hynny y dywedath. wrthynt: Y canhayaf sith amyl ar gweithwyr in anamyl.

Am hyny atolygwch y [arglwyth] y canayaf / thanuon gweithwyr ar eu canayaf.
Kerthwch ymaith: nycha vyvy in ych danuon chwi mal wynymysc bleithieu. Nag

gweithwr y gyfloc.

Simon a Judas Apostolon.
Yr Epistol.
JVdas gwas Ieshu Christ / brawd Iaco / attunt wy a alwyt ac santeithiwyt in
Deo tat / ac a galwyt drwy Jesus Christ: Iud. i.
Trugareth ywch / a thangnethyf a chariat a liowsocker. Caredigion / cymeint
ytoeth vy awyth y escriuenny attoch or iecheit cyffredin / mal na elleis and
escriuenwn attoch can adolwyn ywch cyttri no gyd ar ffyth yr hon a rothet
wnwaith ir saint. Canys e a ymluscath rei annuwiol y mewn / pwy rei a rac
escriuen wit ir varn hon: Y sawl sith in gwady deo yr Arglwyth vnic / ar
Arglwyth einom Jesus Christ. Vy ewyllys i oeth thwyn ar gof i chwi wybot vnwaith
hynn / may yr Arglwyth gwedy itho thwyn y popul in iach allan o tir yr [Aipht /
a thistrywawth eilwers y rei nyd oethynt in credy. Egypt
Ar aggelyon hevyd or ny chatwasant i dechreuad / namyn gady eu trigvan / of ae
goarchatwath mewn catwyne tragyvythawl y dandywyllwc / hyd vrawt y dyth mawr.
Mal am Sodoma a Gomoirha ar dinasoeth oe gogylch / pwy rei in cyfelip voth a
wnayth mi godineb ac aethant ar ol cnawt arall / ynt wedy eu gesot in esam pl /
can o thef poen tan tragyvythawl. Ar un ffynyt y Rei hynn drwy hun ynt in
halogy y cnawt / can thiystyry arglwythiaeth / a chaply y rei sith mewn
awturtot.

Yr Euangel.
HYnn a orchymynnaf ychwi / carry o hanowch eu gylyth. (...)
Os y bid ach casaa / gwythoch gashau o honaw vyvy cynna ych casau
chwchwi. Pe or byt y bysech y byt a garysei yr emo. A chan and ydych or byt /
eithyr my vy ach etholeis allan or byt / am hyny y casha'r byt chwchwi.
Coffewch yr ymadroth a thiwedais wrthych / And yw'r gwas in vwy na eu arglwyth.
Os erlynesont vy vy / wy ach erlynant chwchwi. Os yr ymadroth einof a gatwasant
/ wy a gwatwant yr einowch. Eithyr y pethe hyn oll a wnant wy ychwi er mwyn vy
enw i / can and adnabuont hwn am anuones i. Pe byswn eb thawot ac eb ymthithan
ac wynt / ny bythei arnunt pechat: and yr owi hon nid oes ythynt lliw ymescus
dros eu pechot. Y nep id im cashau i / id in cashay vymtat heuyt. Pe nas gwne
ytheswn i in eu plith wy / y gweithredoeth or nys gwnaeth nep arall / ny bysei
arnunt pechat. Ac yr owrhon y gwelsont / ac wy am casasant mi am tat. Eithyr
(hyn a vu) er cyflowny yr ymadroth sith in escriuenedic in eu cyfreith. Wy am
casasant i in rhat. And gwedy yd el y dithanwr yr hwn a thanuonwy vi ychwi o y
can y tat / is of yspryt gwirioneth (yr hwn a theillia or tat) hwnw a
tystolaytha o hono vi. A chwitheu a testolethwch hevyd / can ych bod or
dechreat y gyd a myvy.

Yr Euangel.
PAn welath Ieshu y minteioeth / e thaeth i vyny ir mynyth: Mat. v.
a gwedy itho eisteth yth aeth eu thiscipulon atto / ac e agores eu eneu ac ae
discawth wy can thoedyt: Gwyn eu byth y tloton in yspryt cans eithynt teyrnas
nef Gwyn eu bid y Rei galarus / canys wynt a thithenir. Gwyn eu byt y Rei
gwaredigenus / canys wynt a vethiannant y thayar. Ewyn eu byt y Rein sith arnun
newyn a sychet cyfiawnder / canys wynt a diwallir. Gwyn e byt y trugarogyon /
canys trugareth a gaffant. Gwyn eu byt y Rei glan o galon / canys wy a welant
Deo. Gwyn eu byt y Rei tangnethyfus / canis wynt eu elwir in plant Deo. Gwyn y
i byt Rei a erlynir er mwyn cyfiawnder: canys eithynt teyrnas neuoeth. Gwynewch
byt pan ych melltithio dynion / ach erlyn a doedyt o gelwyth pop drwc am danoch
er vy mwyni: Byth which lawen a hyfryd / canys mawr yw ych cyfloc in y neuoeth.
Erwyth velly yr erlyuysont ar y prophwyti och blayn chwi. *()*

TERVYN.
A copy of the kings most gracious Privilege.
HEnry the eight by the grace of God King of England France and Ireland,
defender of the faith and of the church of England and Irelande in earth the
supreme head.
To all Driuiers and book cellers, and to other officers, ministers and
subjects,
we do you to understand that of our grace especial, we have granted and given
privilege and license to our well-beloved subjects William Salesbury and Ihon
Waley to print or cause to be printed our book entitled a Dictionarie both
in englshe and welche, whereby our well-beloved subjects in Wales may the sooner
attain and learn our mere english tongue. and that no other person or persons
of what estate degree or condition so ever they be of, do prynte or cause the
same Dictionary to be printed or any part thereof, but only the said William and
Ihon, and either of them, and the assigns of any of them during the space of
seven years next ensuing the first printing of the said Dictionarie. And that
none other person or persons of what estate, degree or condition so ever they
be, do prince or cause to be printed any other book or books which our said
subjects William and Ihon or either of them, hereafter do or shall first
translate and setforth during seven years next ensuing the first printing of
any such book or books. Wherefore we will, and straytly command and charge all
and syngular our subjects, as well printers as book sellers and other persons
within our dominions, that they ne any of them presume to print, or cause to
be printed the said Dictionary or any part thereof, or any other book or
books first translated and printed by the said Wylliam and John or either of
the^ contrary to the meaning of this our present license and privilege upon
pain of our high displeasure.

Given at our Palace of Westminster the.xiii day of December, in the xxxvii
year of our reign.
Imprinted at London by Roberte Crowley for William Salesbury dwelling in Elye
rentes in Holbourne. Anno Domini. M.D.L.I.
